(***************************************************************************************

 Colimits in the slice category of monomorphisms

 Let `C` be a category with a strict initial object. Then we can construct an initial
 object in the slice category of monomorphisms. The construction is the same as the
 construction of initial objects in the slice category.

 The construction of fiberwise coproducts is more interesting. Usually, one is interested
 in the notion of a coherent category in this context. A coherent category is a regular
 category such that subobjects have finite unions. However, while usually one defines
 the subobjects of an object `y` as a quotient of the set of monomorphisms into `y`, one
 does not need to take a quotient if one uses univalent categories. As such, rather than
 defining a notion of coherent category, we give a construct of fiberwise coproducts in
 the slice of monomorphisms if our category satisfies suitable assumptions. These
 assumptions are regularity (so that we have suitable epi-mono factorizations), that
 binary coproducts exists, and that binary coproducts are stable under pullback.

 It is not too difficult to show that fiberwise coproducts exists. To construct the union
 of two monomorphisms, we take the disjoint union of their domain and then we factorize
 the map from the disjoint union as an epimorphism followed by a monomorphism. The main
 difficulty lies in showing that this construction is stable under pullback. Here we use
 that binary coproducts are stable under substitution and that regular epimorphisms are
 stable under substitution.

 Contents
 1. Initial object in the slice of monomorphisms
 2. Binary coproducts in the slice of monomorphisms

 ***************************************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

C: category

 abstract
        (use (InitialArrowEq (O := II))).
Defined.

HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
I: Initial C
HI: is_strict_initial I
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
preserves_initial
  (fiber_functor_from_cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
     HD f)

  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
I: Initial C
HI: is_strict_initial I
∏ x : C, Initial (disp_mono_codomain C)[{x}]
 
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
I: Initial C
HI: is_strict_initial I
x: C
Initial (disp_mono_codomain C)[{x}]

    exact (initial_mono_cod_fib x I HI).
  
C: category
HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving HC: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
I: Initial C
HI: is_strict_initial I
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
preserves_initial
  (fiber_functor_from_cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
     HD f)
 abstract
      (intros x y f z Hz ;
       use to_initial_slice_mono ;
       use (is_initial_mor_to_strict_initial (I ,, HI)) ;
       refine (PullbackPr1 _ · _) ;
       exact (pr11 (InitialArrow
                      (z ,, Hz)
                      (make_mono_in_cat (monic_from_strict_initial I HI _))))).
Defined.

(** * 2. Binary coproducts in the slice of monomorphisms *)
#[local] Opaque regular_category_epi_mono_factorization.

Section BinCoproductsMonoSlice.
  Context {C : category}
          (BC : BinCoproducts C)
          (HC : is_regular_category C)
          {y : C}
          (xf₁ xf₂ : C /m y).

  (**
     Some useful notation
   *)
  Let x₁ : C := mono_cod_dom xf₁.
  Let x₂ : C := mono_cod_dom xf₂.
  Let f₁ : x₁ --> y := mono_cod_mor xf₁.
  Let f₂ : x₂ --> y := mono_cod_mor xf₂.

  Let s : BinCoproduct x₁ x₂ := BC x₁ x₂.

  Definition sum_mor_mono_cod
    : s --> y
    := BinCoproductArrow s f₁ f₂.

  Definition bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod
    : C
    := pr1 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod).

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
Monic C bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod y

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
Monic C bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod y

    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
C ⟦ bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod, y ⟧
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
isMonic ?f

    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
C ⟦ bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod, y ⟧
 exact (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod)).
    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
isMonic
  (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC
            sum_mor_mono_cod))
 exact (pr12 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod))).
  Defined.

  Definition bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod_dom
    : C /m y
    := make_mono_cod_fib_ob bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod.

  (**
     Unions of subobjects as constructed using a epi-mono factorization.
     This is similar to what happens in type theory. If we have two propositions,
     then their disjunction is given as the propositional truncation of their
     disjoint union.
   *)
  Definition bincoproduct_ob_epi
    : s --> bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod
    := pr12 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod).

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
is_regular_epi bincoproduct_ob_epi

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
is_regular_epi bincoproduct_ob_epi

    exact (pr1 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod))).
  Qed.

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C

is_regular_epi bincoproduct_ob_epi

    exact is_regular_epi_bincoproduct_ob_epi.
  Qed.

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C

bincoproduct_ob_epi · bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod =

C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C

x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C

bincoproduct_ob_epi · bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod =
sum_mor_mono_cod

    exact (!(pr22 (pr222 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization HC sum_mor_mono_cod)))).
  Qed.

  Definition bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod
    : C /m y
    := make_mono_cod_fib_ob bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod.

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧

C /m y ⟦ xf₁, bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod ⟧

· mono_cod_mor bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod =

 abstract
        (rewrite !assoc' ;
         etrans ; [ apply maponpaths ; apply bincoproduct_ob_comm | ] ;
         apply BinCoproductIn1Commutes).
  Defined.

f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
?g · mono_cod_mor bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod =
mono_cod_mor xf₂

C ⟦ mono_cod_dom xf₂,
mono_cod_dom bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod ⟧
 exact (BinCoproductIn2 s · bincoproduct_ob_epi).

BC: BinCoproducts C

· mono_cod_mor bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod =
mono_cod_mor xf₂
 abstract
        (rewrite !assoc' ;
         etrans ; [ apply maponpaths ; apply bincoproduct_ob_comm | ] ;
         apply BinCoproductIn2Commutes).
  Defined.

  Section UMP.
    Context {gz : C /m y}
            (φp : xf₁ --> gz)
            (ψq : xf₂ --> gz).

    Let z : C := mono_cod_dom gz.
    Let g : z --> y := mono_cod_mor gz.
    Let φ : x₁ --> z := mono_dom_mor φp.
    Let ψ : x₂ --> z := mono_dom_mor ψq.

    Definition mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_from_sum
      : s --> mono_cod_dom gz
      := BinCoproductArrow s φ ψ.

    Let ζ := mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_from_sum.

    Qed.

    Let fact : ∑ (l : bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod --> mono_cod_dom gz),
               l · mono_cod_mor gz
               =
               bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod
               ×
               bincoproduct_ob_epi · l = ζ
      := pr1 (is_strong_epi_bincoproduct_ob_epi
                (mono_cod_dom gz)
                y
                (mono_cod_mor gz)
                ζ
                bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod
                mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor_eq
                (MonicisMonic _ _)).

    Definition mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor
      : mono_cod_dom bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod --> mono_cod_dom gz
      := pr1 fact.

    Let l := mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor.

    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
gz: C /m y
φp: C /m y ⟦ xf₁, gz ⟧
ψq: C /m y ⟦ xf₂, gz ⟧
z:= mono_cod_dom gz: C
g:= mono_cod_mor gz: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
φ:= mono_dom_mor φp: C ⟦ x₁, z ⟧
ψ:= mono_dom_mor ψq: C ⟦ x₂, z ⟧
ζ:= mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_from_sum: C ⟦ s, mono_cod_dom gz ⟧
fact:= pr1
(is_strong_epi_bincoproduct_ob_epi (mono_cod_dom gz) y (mono_cod_mor gz) ζ
bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor_eq
(MonicisMonic C (mono_cod_mor gz))): ∑
l : C ⟦ bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod,
    mono_cod_dom gz ⟧,
l · mono_cod_mor gz =
bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod
× bincoproduct_ob_epi · l = ζ
l:= mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor: C ⟦ mono_cod_dom bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod,
mono_cod_dom gz ⟧
l · mono_cod_mor gz = bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod

BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧
f₂:= mono_cod_mor xf₂: C ⟦ x₂, y ⟧
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
gz: C /m y
φp: C /m y ⟦ xf₁, gz ⟧
ψq: C /m y ⟦ xf₂, gz ⟧
z:= mono_cod_dom gz: C
g:= mono_cod_mor gz: C ⟦ z, y ⟧
φ:= mono_dom_mor φp: C ⟦ x₁, z ⟧
ψ:= mono_dom_mor ψq: C ⟦ x₂, z ⟧
ζ:= mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_from_sum: C ⟦ s, mono_cod_dom gz ⟧
fact:= pr1
(is_strong_epi_bincoproduct_ob_epi (mono_cod_dom gz) y (mono_cod_mor gz) ζ
bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor_eq
(MonicisMonic C (mono_cod_mor gz))): ∑
l : C ⟦ bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod,
    mono_cod_dom gz ⟧,
l · mono_cod_mor gz =
bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod
× bincoproduct_ob_epi · l = ζ
l:= mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor: C ⟦ mono_cod_dom bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod,
mono_cod_dom gz ⟧
l · mono_cod_mor gz = bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod

      exact (pr12 fact).
    Qed.

    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HC: is_regular_category C
y: C
xf₁, xf₂: C /m y
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xf₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xf₂: C
f₁:= mono_cod_mor xf₁: C ⟦ x₁, y ⟧

C /m y ⟦ bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod, gz ⟧

     (mono_cod_dom gz) y

× bincoproduct_ob_epi · l = ζ

mono_cod_dom gz ⟧
?g · mono_cod_mor gz =

 apply mor_from_mono_cod_bincoproduct_mor_eq1.
    Defined.
  End UMP.
End BinCoproductsMonoSlice.

Section BinCoproductsStable.
  Context {C : category}
          (BC : BinCoproducts C)
          (HBC : stable_bincoproducts BC)
          (HC : is_regular_category C)
          {y₁ y₂ : C}
          {f : y₁ --> y₂}
          (xg₁ xg₂ : C /m y₂).

  Let PB : Pullbacks C := is_regular_category_pullbacks HC.
  Let HD : cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C) := mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB.

  (**
     We start by introducing some notation that we use.

     Concretely, our goal is to make the following diagram

<<
        f^*(x₁ + x₂) --> f^* x₁ + f^* x₂ --> im_f
               |                              |
               |                              |
               V                              V
           f^*(im) ------------------------>  y₁
>>

     Here `im` is the image of `x₁ + x₂ --> y₂`
     and `im_f` is the image of `f^* x₁ + f^* x₂ --> y₁`.
     We use the notation `f^*` for pullback along `f`.

     By showing that the map `f^*(x₁ + x₂) --> f^*(im)` is a strong epimorphism
     and that `im_f --> y'_1` is mono, we get the desired morphisms as a lift.
   *)

  Let x₁ : C := mono_cod_dom xg₁.
  Let x₂ : C := mono_cod_dom xg₂.
  Let g₁ : x₁ --> y₂ := mono_cod_mor xg₁.
  Let g₂ : x₂ --> y₂ := mono_cod_mor xg₂.

  Let im : C := bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂.
  Let s : BinCoproduct x₁ x₂ := BC x₁ x₂.
  Let e : s --> im := bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂.
  Let m : im --> y₂ := bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂.

  Let sum : C / y₂ := make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂).

  Let fx₁ : C := mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁).
  Let fx₂ : C := mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂).
  Let fg₁ : fx₁ --> y₁ := mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁).
  Let fg₂ : fx₂ --> y₁ := mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂).

  Let im_f : C
    := bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂).

  Let sf : BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂ := BC fx₁ fx₂.
  Let ef : sf --> im_f := bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC _ _.
  Let mf : Monic _ im_f y₁ := bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC _ _.

  Let sumf : C / y₁
    := make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)).

  (**
     Now we define some more maps in the desired diagram.
     We start with the map `f^*(im) --> y₁`, which we call `f_e_im`

     The reason why this morphism exists, is because we constructed
     `f^*(im)` as the following pullback

<<
      f^*(im) --------> im
        |               |
        |               |
        V               V
        y₁ -----------> y₂
>>
   *)
  Let im_m_slice : C/y₂ := make_cod_fib_ob m.
  Let f_im : C := cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice).
  Let f_e_im : f_im --> y₁ := cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice).

  (**
     Next we construct the map `f^*(x₁ + x₂) --> f^*(im)`.
     This map exists by the functoriality of taking the pullback.
     We call this map `f_epi`.
   *)
  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
C / y₂ ⟦ sum, im_m_slice ⟧

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C

g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
C / y₂ ⟦ sum, im_m_slice ⟧

BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C

C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
?g · cod_mor im_m_slice = cod_mor sum

 exact e.

 apply bincoproduct_ob_comm.
  Defined.

  Local Definition f_epi
    : cod_dom (cod_pb PB f sum) --> f_im
    := dom_mor (#(cod_pb PB f) sum_im_map).

  (**
     Finally, we construct the map `f^*(x₁ + x₂) --> f^* x₁ + f^* x₂`.
     This map exists since we assume coproducts are stable under pullback.
   *)

  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁

  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁

CP:= make_BinCoproduct (C / y₁)
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
  (cod_pb PB f
     (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
        (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
        (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn1
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn2
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (from_stable BC PB HBC f
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)): BinCoproduct
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
C / y₁ ⟦ cod_pb PB f sum, sumf ⟧

           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn2
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (from_stable BC PB HBC f
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)): BinCoproduct
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
C / y₁ ⟦ cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂),
sumf ⟧

        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn2
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (from_stable BC PB HBC f
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)): BinCoproduct
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
C / y₁ ⟦ cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂),
sumf ⟧

     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁

  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
  (cod_pb PB f
     (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
        (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
        (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn1
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (# (cod_pb PB f)
     (BinCoproductIn2
        (bincoproducts_cod_fib y₂ BC
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
           (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))))
  (from_stable BC PB HBC f
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁)
     (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)): BinCoproduct
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₁))
  (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
(λ ff : C
        ⟦ pr1
            (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂)),
        pr1 sumf ⟧,
 ff · pr2 sumf =
 pr2 (cod_pb PB f (mono_cod_to_cod_fib y₂ xg₂))
 · identity y₁)
  (BinCoproductIn2
     (BC (mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁))
        (mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂))))
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           unfold sum_mor_mono_cod ;
           rewrite BinCoproductIn2Commutes ;
           rewrite id_right ;
           apply idpath).
  Defined.

  (**
     We can show that the desired diagram commutes
   *)

HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC

y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C

(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂

  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧

f_epi · f_e_im = dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef · mf

im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
cod_mor (cod_pb PB f sum) =
dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef · mf

    exact (mor_eq stable_pb_sum_map).
  Qed.

  (**
     Note that we need that `f_epi` is a strong epimorphism.
     To see why, first note that we have the following diagram

<<
      f^*(x₁ + x₂) ---> x₁ + x₂
        |                  |
        |                  |
        V                  V
      f^*(im) -----------> im
        |                  |
        |                  |
        V                  V
        y₁ ------------->  y₂
>>

     In this digram, both the lower and the whole square are pullback squares.
     Hence, the upper square is a pullback square as well.
     Since our category is regular, we have that regular epis are stable under pullbacks,
     and thus `f_epi` is a regular epi.
   *)
  Local Definition left_map
    : f_im --> bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂
    := PullbackPr1 (PB _ _ _ m f).

  Local Definition top_map
    : cod_dom (cod_pb PB f sum) --> BC x₁ x₂
    := PullbackPr1 _.

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
top_map · bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂ =
dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map)
· left_map

  
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂

g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
top_map · bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂ =
dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map)
· left_map

  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
PullbackPr1
  (PB y₂ (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
     (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f) · e =
top_map · bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  Section UMP.
    Context {w : C}
            {h : w --> BC x₁ x₂}
            {k : w --> f_im}
            (p : h · e = k · left_map).

    Let P : Pullback (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f
      := PB _ _ _ (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f.
    Let Q : Pullback m f := PB _ _ _ m f.

sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C

fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧

  (λ x : C ⟦ w, cod_dom (cod_pb PB f sum) ⟧,
   x · top_map = h
   × x
     · dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map) =
     k)

        intro ; apply isapropdirprod ; apply homset_property.

      (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map) = k
r: pr1 ζ₁
· PullbackArrow
    (PB y₂ im y₁
       (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                 HC (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂)))
       f)
    (PB y₂
       (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂))
       y₁ (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f)
    (PullbackPr1
       (PB y₂
          (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁)
             (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
          (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f) · e)
    (PullbackPr2
       (PB y₂
          (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁)
             (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
          (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f))
    (cod_fiber_functor_pb_subproof PB y₁ y₂ f sum
       im_m_slice sum_im_map)
· PullbackPr2
    (PB y₂ im y₁
       (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                 HC (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂)))
       f) =
pr1 ζ₂
· PullbackArrow
    (PB y₂ im y₁
       (pr122 (regular_category_epi_mono_factorization
                 HC (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂)))
       f)
    (PB y₂
       (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂))
       y₁ (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f)

y₁, y₂: C

x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, BC x₁ x₂ ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, f_im ⟧
p: h · e = k · left_map
P:= PB y₂ (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f: Pullback (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f
Q:= PB y₂ im y₁ m f: Pullback m f
h · sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂ =
k · cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice) · f
 abstract
          (unfold left_map in p ;
           pose proof (maponpaths (λ z, z · m) p) as q ;
           simpl in q ;
           rewrite !assoc' in q ;
           refine (maponpaths (λ z, h · z) (!_) @ q @ _) ;
           [ apply bincoproduct_ob_comm | ] ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           apply maponpaths ;
           apply PullbackSqrCommutes).
    Defined.

  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, BC x₁ x₂ ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, f_im ⟧
p: h · e = k · left_map
P:= PB y₂ (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f: Pullback (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f
Q:= PB y₂ im y₁ m f: Pullback m f
is_regular_epi_f_epi_map
· dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map)
· PullbackPr2 (PB y₂ im y₁ m f) =
k · PullbackPr2 (PB y₂ im y₁ m f)

BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, BC x₁ x₂ ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, f_im ⟧
p: h · e = k · left_map
P:= PB y₂ (BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂)) y₁
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f: Pullback (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂) f
Q:= PB y₂ im y₁ m f: Pullback m f
is_regular_epi_f_epi_map
· PullbackPr1 (PB y₂ (pr1 sum) y₁ (pr2 sum) f)
· pr1 sum_im_map = k · PullbackPr1 (PB y₂ im y₁ m f)

Q:= PB y₂ im y₁ m f: Pullback m f

  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁

  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)

im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
top_map · bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂ =
dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map)
· left_map
 exact pb_sqr_commutes.

hk · top_map = h
× hk · dom_mor (cod_fiber_functor_pb PB f sum_im_map) =
  k

HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
w: C
h: C ⟦ w, BC (mono_cod_dom xg₁) (mono_cod_dom xg₂) ⟧
k: C ⟦ w, f_im ⟧
p: h · bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂ =
k · left_map
is_regular_epi_f_epi_map p · top_map = h
 abstract
            (exact (PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1 _ _ _ _ _)).

  (**
     This allows us to construct the desired lift.
   *)
  Let ℓ : f_im --> im_f
    := pr11 (is_regular_epi_f_epi _ _ _ _ _ diagram_commutes (MonicisMonic _ _)).

  Let ℓl : ℓ · mf = f_e_im
    := pr121 (is_regular_epi_f_epi _ _ _ _ _ diagram_commutes (MonicisMonic _ _)).
  Let ℓr : f_epi · ℓ = dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef
    := pr221 (is_regular_epi_f_epi _ _ _ _ _ diagram_commutes (MonicisMonic _ _)).

⟦ mono_cod_dom
    (mono_cod_pb PB f
       (bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂)),
mono_cod_dom
  (bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod BC HC
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)) ⟧
 exact ℓ.
    
C: category
BC: BinCoproducts C
HBC: stable_bincoproducts BC
HC: is_regular_category C
y₁, y₂: C
f: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
xg₁, xg₂: C /m y₂
PB:= is_regular_category_pullbacks HC: Pullbacks C
HD:= mono_cod_disp_cleaving PB: cleaving (disp_mono_codomain C)
x₁:= mono_cod_dom xg₁: C
x₂:= mono_cod_dom xg₂: C
g₁:= mono_cod_mor xg₁: C ⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
g₂:= mono_cod_mor xg₂: C ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
im:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C
s:= BC x₁ x₂: BinCoproduct x₁ x₂
e:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ s, im ⟧
m:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂: C ⟦ im, y₂ ⟧
sum:= make_cod_fib_ob (sum_mor_mono_cod BC xg₁ xg₂): C / y₂
fx₁:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C
fx₂:= mono_cod_dom (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
fg₁:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁): C ⟦ fx₁, y₁ ⟧
fg₂:= mono_cod_mor (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ fx₂, y₁ ⟧
im_f:= bincoproduct_ob_dom_mono_cod BC HC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
(mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C
sf:= BC fx₁ fx₂: BinCoproduct fx₁ fx₂
ef:= bincoproduct_ob_epi BC HC 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): C ⟦ sf, im_f ⟧
mf:= bincoproduct_ob_mor_mono_cod BC HC
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) 
  (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂): Monic C im_f y₁
sumf:= make_cod_fib_ob
  (sum_mor_mono_cod BC (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁)
     (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)): C / y₁
im_m_slice:= make_cod_fib_ob m: C / y₂
f_im:= cod_dom (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C
f_e_im:= cod_mor (cod_pb PB f im_m_slice): C ⟦ f_im, y₁ ⟧
ℓ:= pr11 (is_regular_epi_f_epi im_f y₁ mf
        (dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef) f_e_im
        diagram_commutes 
        (MonicisMonic C mf)): C ⟦ f_im, im_f ⟧
ℓl:= pr121 (is_regular_epi_f_epi im_f y₁ mf
         (dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef) f_e_im
         diagram_commutes 
         (MonicisMonic C mf)): ℓ · mf = f_e_im
ℓr:= pr221 (is_regular_epi_f_epi im_f y₁ mf
         (dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef) f_e_im
         diagram_commutes 
         (MonicisMonic C mf)): f_epi · ℓ = dom_mor stable_pb_sum_map · ef
ℓ
· mono_cod_mor
    (bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod BC HC
       (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₁) (mono_cod_pb PB f xg₂)) =
mono_cod_mor
  (mono_cod_pb PB f
     (bincoproduct_ob_mono_cod BC HC xg₁ xg₂))
 exact ℓl.
  Defined.
End BinCoproductsStable.

               (pr1 (HD Γ₂ Γ₁ s ψ))
